Broo

Chapter Four: On the Ornaments of the Vaiс╣гс╣Зava

┬╣Having once bathed in the supreme T─лrtha by the name of ┼Ъr─л Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa Caitanya, even the perpetually unclean becomes the best of the clean and fit to speak on Svadharma.

DDс╣м: Thinking that reciting the name of the Lord is more purifying than even this kind of bathing [described in the previous chapter], and also that this causes even himself, who is unqualified, to become eligible for writing on Bhagavad Dharma, the author writes this verse. Even once bathed in the supreme T─лrtha of the name тАЬ┼Ъr─л Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa CaitanyaтАЭ means have once recited that name. Perpetually unclean: a person who through birth and so on is supremely impure becomes the best of clean persons and fit to speak, eligible to teach. This is the meaning.

┬▓Now one should return to oneтАЩs home and first bow to oneтАЩs chosen Lord, the preceptors and the elders, except those carrying flowers, firewood, Ku┼Ыa grass and water.

[тАж]. This is also stated in the Bс╣Ыhann─Бrad─лya Pur─Бс╣Зa, in connection with Sad─Бc─Бra (23.40): тАЬAlso, one should not greet those that are bathing, bringing firewood and flowers, carrying a waterpot or eating.тАЭ[^FNB000406]

As also in the Nс╣Ыsiс╣Гha Pur─Бс╣Зa (58.92cdтАУ93ab):[^FNB000407]

┬│Having bowed to the god in the water, he should go home and then worship Viс╣гс╣Зu with the Puruс╣гa hymn.[^FNB000408]

Cleaning the LordтАЩs Temple

тБ┤After doing ─Аcamana and so on, one should cleanse Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs temple. Seeing and glorifying Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, one should offer him oneтАЩs self as his servant. тБ╡Bringing pure cow dung, clay and water, one should devotedly smear it all around and sprinkle its yard as well.

It refers to the temple of Viс╣гс╣Зu. One should sprinkle its yard as well.

This is also mentioned in the story of Ambar─лс╣гa in the Ninth Book (BhP9.4.28):[^FNB000409]

тБ╢He engaged his mind in the lotus feet of Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa,

his words in describing the qualities of Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha,

his hands at cleansing HariтАЩs temple, and so on,

his ears in the rising of AcyutaтАЩs noble stories.

The words and so on refer to acts such as smearing. He set his listening or ears on the rising or appearance of hearing the noble stories of Acyuta.

And in the Eleventh Book, in the discussion between the Lord and Uddhava concerning Bhagavad Dharma (BhP11.11.39):

тБ╖One should attend to my house like a servant, free from deceit, by cleaning, smearing and moistening and by drawing Maс╣Зс╕Нalas.

Cleaning means removing dust and smearing plastering with cow dung, water and so on. Moistening means sprinkling with it. Drawing Maс╣Зс╕Нalas refers to fashioning the Sarvatobhadra and other diagrams. Attend to my house means cleaning my abode.

тБ╕One who regularly cleans the house of Narasiс╣Гha is freed from all sins and delights in the world of Viс╣гс╣Зu.

In the Viс╣гс╣Зudharmottara Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

тБ╣That man who cleans the abode of Ke┼Ыava is cleansed from Rajas and TamasтАФthere is no doubt about it. ┬╣тБ░O king! The man who cleans will easily go to heaven and delight there for as many years as the specks of dust that he cleaned away.

Broo

In the Var─Бha Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000411]

┬╣┬╣One will be honoured in ┼Ъ─Бkadv─лpa[^FNB000412] for as many thousands of years as the strokes one gives in cleaning the earth.

Using the neuter gender for the word stroke is an archaic irregularity.[^FNB000413] [тАж] The word earth can also be analyzed as a separate word, meaning тАЬO earth!тАЭ.[^FNB000414]

┬╣┬▓One is also born as my devotee, endowed with all virtues, clean, a pure Bh─Бgavata, free from all offences. ┬╣┬│Then, having enjoyed all pleasures, one will cross over the ocean of birth and death, and after falling from ┼Ъ─Бkadv─лpa, one will go to heaven. ┬╣тБ┤Dwelling in the Nandana forest, one will enjoy with Apsaras, and after falling from Nandana, one who sticks to my work will give up all attachment and go to my world.

One who sticks to my work means one who is fixed in devotion to me.

The Greatness of Plastering

In the same book:[^FNB000415]

┬╣тБ╡One who fetches cow dung and smears the ground of my dwelling will be born as my devotee for as many thousands of years as the number of steps he takes in smearing all around there.

[тАж] Using the masculine gender for the word steps is an archaic irregularity.

Broo

lidv─лpa,[^FNB000416] he will become a virtuous king and then be born as my devotee, expert in all the scriptures. ┬╣тБ╕And when I see someone of fixed vows who smears the ground with cow dung, I am pleased with that plastering. ┬╣тБ╣And the cow with whose dung the earth is smeared is by only one act of plastering completely freed from that birth as a cow.

[тАж]. That cow is completely, especially and powerfully freed, that is, it attains Goloka.

┬▓тБ░O fortunate one, listen to the truth of the full merit of one who gives water for plastering the ground of my place! ┬▓┬╣Beautiful one, he will be honoured in heaven for as many thousands of years as there are drops of water in the plastering. ┬▓┬▓O earth, he will be honoured in Krau├▒cadv─лpa[^FNB000417] for as many thousands of years as there are drops in the water. ┬▓┬│After falling from Krau├▒cadv─лpa, one will be devoted to all virtues, give up all attachment and go to my world.

[тАж] And afterwards, when one has fallen from heaven, one will go to Krau├▒cadv─лpa and be honoured there. The meaning is that one will be revered by the inhabitants there.

Broo

In the Viс╣гс╣Зudharmottara Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬▓тБ┤That man who regularly plasters the dwelling of Viс╣гс╣Зu with cow dung will easily go to auspicious worlds. ┬▓тБ╡O king, one who plasters one cubit of ground will become a king in heaven and get a hundred of divine beauties.

And in the Nс╣Ыsiс╣Гha Pur─Бс╣Зa (33.14):[^FNB000418]

┬▓тБ╢One who plasters with cow dung, clay and water attains the fruit of the Candr─Бyaс╣Зa sacrifice and is honoured in the world of Viс╣гс╣Зu.

In the instructions to the messengers of Dharmar─Бja in the same book (тАУ):[^FNB000419]

┬▓тБ╖Stay away from the three families of one who cleans the abode of Viс╣гс╣Зu and plasters it with cow dung!

Let alone the removal of the sins and so on for the one who plasters, the author gives this verse to indicate that the same will happen to his relatives as well. The three families refer to the family of the father, the family of the mother and the family of the wife.

The Greatness of Sprinkling

In the Viс╣гс╣Зudharmottara Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000420]

┬▓тБ╕One who sprinkles water in the abode of a god stills his afflictionsтАФdo not doubt this. ┬▓тБ╣The man who sprinkles in the house of the God of gods is freed from all his sins and enjoys the world of Varuс╣Зa.

Broo

┬│тБ░Skilfully one should draw Sarvatobhadras, lotuses, Svastikas and so on, and then decorate the temple of Hari variously.

This is mentioned in the Narasiс╣Гha Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000421]

┬│┬╣By cleaning and plastering and by colourful lotuses and so on should one happily beautify great Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs temple and its splendid parts.

Colourful lotuses means drawings of various colours and lotuses, or else lotuses made of powder dyes of different hues. And so on means Svastikas and similar figures. The splendid parts refer to walls, fences and so on. The meaning is that one should decorate them as well. Or else it is an adverb, but the meaning will be the same.

The Greatness of Maс╣Зс╕Нalas

In connection with the month of K─Бrttika in the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000422]

┬│┬▓All of the sin of approaching one not to be approached and eating what is not be eaten is destroyed when one decorates the house of Hari. ┬│┬│One who with mud and mineral colours makes a Maс╣Зс╕Нala the size of minute size in front of Ke┼Ыava will stay in heaven for a hundred Kalpas. ┬│тБ┤But one who makes a beautiful Svastika in front of the ┼Ъ─Бlagr─Бma stone, especially in the month of K─Бrttika, purifies seven generations of the family. ┬│тБ╡That woman who regularly makes a Maс╣Зс╕Нala in front of Ke┼Ыava will not become a widow for seven lifetimes.

Maс╣Зс╕Нala refers to the Sarvatobhadra and others. [тАж]

┬│тБ╢She who fetches cow dung and makes a Maс╣Зс╕Нala in front of Ke┼Ыava will never be separated from her husband, children or wealth. ┬│тБ╖One who decorates the courtyard of the God of gods with pictures and Svastikas will enjoy in the three worlds.

Broo

In the N─Бrada Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬│тБ╕That man who smears with clay, mineral colours, pigments or cow dung will be borne in a celestial chariot.

Smears means who also makes Maс╣Зс╕Нalas and so on.

And in the Haribhaktisudhodaya (20.77):

┬│тБ╣The happy man who smears Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs abode and decorates it with colours is lovingly beheld by the inhabitants of the world of Viс╣гс╣Зu.

Characteristics of a Svastika

In the ─Аgama:[^FNB000423]

тБ┤тБ░Having divided the squares in the intermediate directions into sixteen parts, one should wipe away to make a svastika form, with white, yellow, red and blue.[^FNB000424]

About this, there is also a statement in the Pa├▒car─Бtra:[^FNB000425]

тБ┤┬╣For Maс╣Зс╕Нalas, one should make use of dyes of five colour: white using rice powder or that of barley; тБ┤┬▓red, from saffron, vermillion, red chalk or the like; yellow, from orpiment or from turmeric; blue, from burned green barley; and the mixture from blue and yellow.

One gets white and the other colours from powders and the blue colour from burned green barley. When that is mixed with yellow one gets the colour green. This is the meaning.[^FNB000426] These are said to be the five colours.

Broo

Hoisting Flags, Banners and so on There

тБ┤┬│Then a man with devotion to the Lord should raise flags, banners and so on at the temple of Hari and decorate it in various ways.

[тАж]

The Greatness of Hoisting Flags

In a discussion between M─Бrkaс╣Зс╕Нeya and Indradyumna in the Greatness of Dv─Бrak─Б in the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (7.4.23.61):[^FNB000427]

тБ┤тБ┤One who devotedly raises a flag over the temple will have a dwelling in Brahm─БтАЩs world and enjoy along with Brahm─Б.

In the Bс╣Ыhann─Бrad─лya Pur─Бс╣Зa (18.3):

тБ┤тБ╡One who raises an excellent flag over the dwelling of Viс╣гс╣Зu will be honoured by Brahm─Б and the othersтАФwhat is the use of many other words?

And also later in the same book (18.46тАУ47, 49):[^FNB000428]

тБ┤тБ╢Best of Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, as long as the cloth of the flag flutters in the wind, so long all sins are destroyed: there is no doubt about it. тБ┤тБ╖One may possess the great sins or all different sins but when one has raised a flag at Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs house one is liberated from it all. тБ┤тБ╕Even the virtuous people who simply see the raised flag and delight in it are immediately freed from millions of minor sins.

тБ┤тБ╣Now, whatever else of the wonderful greatness of hoisting the flag that is explained in the Bс╣Ыhann─Бrad─лya Pur─Бс╣Зa should be considered in its entirety here.[^FNB000429]

The Greatness of Hoisting Banners

In the same place of the section on the greatness of Dv─Бrak─Б (тАУ):

тБ╡тБ░One who adorns Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs dwelling with banners will always dwell in his abode and nowhere else.

In the Viс╣гс╣Зudharmottara Pur─Бс╣Зa (3.341.57тАУ58):

тБ╡┬╣That Br─Бhmaс╣Зa who donates a beautiful banner to the dwelling of Ke┼Ыava attains the world of V─Бyu for many years. тБ╡┬▓As long as it flutters in the wind above the house of Ke┼Ыava will all his sins will be blown away from his body.

The Greatness of Raising Festoons of Leaves and the Trunks of Banana Trees

In the same place of the Greatness of Dv─Бrak─Б (Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa 7.4.23.60, 59ab):[^FNB000430]

тБ╡┬│O king, one who arranges for a festoon of leaves for Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs dwelling will be attended by thousands of the best of gods and goddesses. тБ╡тБ┤The king of gods along with the Apsarases bid welcome the one who decorates Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs house with banana tree trunks.

Above (4.43) the author wrote that one should offer flags, banners and so on. In these two verses, he describes the greatness of offering items such as festoons of leaves that are included within that and so on. They bid, greet him, so that he is made welcome, or then [nandate means] that they rejoice. Or else, they greet his auspicious arrival. Another reading has тАЬhonourтАЭ [instead of bid welcome].

Cleaning the Seat, Vessels, Clothes and so on

тБ╡тБ╡Whatever copper vessels or whatever clothes, seats and so on there are that belong to the Lord, should all be cleaned in the proper way.

touched by the leavings of ┼Ъ┼лdras, they are purified threefold by water and sour ashes.

The word тАЬvesselsтАЭ should be supplied. Made of gems refers to things fashioned of crystal and so on. [тАж] Unsmeared means that they are without the dirt of food and so on. [тАж] Even though the LordтАЩs vessels are never touched by the leavings of ┼Ъ┼лdras, still, by mistake or carelessness that might happen, and therefore their purification is given.[^FNB000433] The same applies in all the cases below as well. Threefold means three times. [тАж]

тБ╢┬╣Very contaminated vessels should not be used for Hari again after they have been purified but be set down for oneself instead. тБ╢┬▓Once they have been cleaned, very contaminated vessels should be used for hospitality or be exchanged for some other work for the Master. тБ╢┬│In the case of exchanging, another vessel should be offered to the Lord. Everywhere in the world this is known as the correct conduct.

Manu (5.114):[^FNB000434]

тБ╢тБ┤Copper, iron, bell metal, brass, tin and lead items should be properly cleaned with alkali, acid and water.

Properly means until the impurity is removed. [тАж] Among these, acid should be used for copper and alkali for the others, but water should be supplied in both cases. This is the meaning, as it was said properly.

┼Ъaс╣Еkha (16.3cdтАУ4ab):[^FNB000435]

тБ╢тБ╡Copper, lead and tin should be purified with sour water; alkali has been set down for bell metal and iron.

рдкреНрд░рдХреНрд╖реЗрдкреНрддрд╡реНрдпрд╛рдирд┐198 рддрд╛рдиреНрдпреН рдЕрдЧреНрдиреМ рдпрдЪреН рдЪ рдпрд╛рд╡рддреН рд╕рд╣реЗрджреН рдЕрдкрд┐ \ред\редремрео\ред\ред

Broo

The author demonstrates the above statement [on the division of cleaning agents] with this verse.

Further:

тБ╢тБ╢A vessel touched by the leavings of a woman lying in, by alcohol or the like becomes pure by cleansing three times seven, but not bell metal: heating.

All the previous examples refer to insignificant pollution. Verses66тАУ68 describe purification in cases of major pollution.[^FNB000436] A woman lying in means a woman who has just given birth and not yet undergone purification. Alternatively, it refers to a midwife. Touched by the leavings means that the leavings of this person have touched it, or else that she has eaten off it. A vessel refers to a metallic vessel by the strength of the context. Or the like refers to blood and so on. The meaning of three times seven is cleansing twenty-one times. But some say: тАЬPurity is achieved by cleaning three times each with seven powders: that of barley, wheat, Kal─Бya beans and so on.тАЭ But a plate of bell metal is not purified in this way, instead it needs heating or scorching. The meaning of the reading тАЬplateтАЭ is obvious.[^FNB000437]

And elsewhere:

тБ╢тБ╖Copper is purified by acid, but not if smeared with meat. That which has been smeared by meat is purified by reheating.

In the Brahma Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000438]

тБ╢тБ╕And items touched by a woman lying in, a corpse, faeces, urine or a menstruating woman should be thrown into a fire for as much as they can bear it.

рдПрддрдЪреН216 рдЪрд╛рд▓реНрдкреЛрдкрд╣рддреМ рдЕрддреНрдпрдиреНрддреЛрдкрд╣рддреМ217 рдЪ рдореГрдиреНрдордпрдВ рддреНрдпрд╛рдЬреНрдпрдореН рдПрд╡реЗрддрд┐ рд▓рд┐рдЦрддрд┐ рдорджреНрдпреИрд░реН рдЗрддрд┐ \ред рд╖реНрдареАрд╡рдиреИрдГ рд▓рд╛рд▓рд╛рдкреНрд░рдХреНрд╖реЗрдкреИрдГ \ред рдкрд╛рдард╛рдиреНрддрд░рдВ рд╕реНрдкрд╖реНрдЯрдореН \ред\редренрез\ред\ред

Broo

In this verse, the author gives details about heating. [тАж] Here, being touched by a woman who is lying in or menstruating means having come into contact with her leavings or her having eaten from them. The word ┼Ыava [corpse] can also be read as s─Бva, with a dental s, meaning ─Бsava or alcohol.[^FNB000439] As much as: the particular material should be thrown into as hot a fire or for as long a time as that particular material can bear it. This is the meaning.

For this reason, Devala says (тАУ):[^FNB000440]

тБ╢тБ╣Metal items are purified by heating, by ashes or by cow dung; stone items by heating, burying or by water. тБ╖тБ░Wooden items are purified by paring and by water, mud and cow dung and clay vessels are said to be purified by heating.

The author now invokes the statement of Devala about all of this which has been more or less said already. Metal items refer to vessels made of ingredients such as gold. By heating if the pollution is major; otherwise by ashes and so on. This is the meaning. Similar cases later on should be understood in the same way. Burying refers to digging up the ground and placing them in it for a week or longer depending on the type of contamination. [тАж] Heating means baking them again. This is also stated by Y─Бj├▒avalkya (1.187): тАЬClay items by baking againтАЭ.

Manu (5.123):[^FNB000441]

тБ╖┬╣When a clay item has been touched by alcohol, urine, faeces, mucus, pus, bone or spittle it cannot be purified by baking again.

The author gives this verse to show that the above case refers to insignificant pollution and that in the case of major pollution, clay items should be discarded. Spittle refers to excretion of saliva. The other reading is clear.[^FNB000442]

Broo

The elder ┼Ъ─Бt─Бtapa (тАУ):[^FNB000443]

тБ╖┬▓But among conjoined vessels, purification is mandated only for the one that is contaminated: the cleansing of vessels is joint.

Conjoined vessels means vessels that are in contact, connecting with each other. The purification that has been given applies to that one alone, not to those others that are touching it. This is the meaning.[^FNB000444] In the different reading, the cleansing of vessels is joint means that the cleansing of one object effects the cleansing of all the other objects as well. Therefore ┼Ъ─Бt─Бtapa also says (тАУ):[^FNB000445] тАЬOnly one that touches impurity is contaminated; another one who touches that is not contaminated. This is the rule for all items.тАЭ[^FNB000446]

Clothes and so on

┼Ъaс╣Еkha (тАУ):[^FNB000447]

тБ╖┬│Woven cloth that has become soiled should first be cleaned with water and alkali and then be replaced after drying in the sun or in the wind. тБ╖тБ┤When only lightly contaminated, wool, silk, muslin, linen, bark fibre cloth, sheep wool and skins are cleansed by drying, sprinkling and so on. тБ╖тБ╡When they have become smeared with something impure, they should be cleaned thoroughly with white mustard, flour, powdered Pal─Б┼Ыa leaves (Butea Frondosa) and the juice of fruits and bark. тБ╖тБ╢Wagtail and other cushions and garments of flowers and gems should be dried in the sun and then again rubbed a little with the hand, тБ╖тБ╖after which they are sprinkled with water and then said to be clean. Also such items should be cleaned in the above way if they have been smeared with great impurity.

Broo

wool and sheep wool is that they are made from the hair of different animals or because they are different substances.[^FNB000448] [тАж] Garments of flowers and gems refer to garments made of painted flowers and garments beautified with gold paint and gems.

┼Ъ─Бt─Бtapa (тАУ):

тБ╖тБ╕Even when touched by a Caс╣Зс╕Н─Бla, cloths coloured with safflower, saffron or with red lac are purified by sprinkling.

[тАж] By a Caс╣Зс╕Н─Бla implies any other kind of untouchable as well. [тАж]

Yama (тАУ):[^FNB000449]

тБ╖тБ╣The skin of a black antelope by the wind; chowries, by mud and water; bone and teeth, by cow urine; linen cloth, by white mustard seeds.

[тАж] Bone refers to conches and so on, teeth to ivory and so on.

┼Ъaс╣Еkha (16.10):[^FNB000450]

тБ╕тБ░And things made of teeth and horn, by the paste of white mustard seeds; vessels made of fruits, by cowsтАЩ hair; and in the case of bone, as for horn.

Vessels made of fruits means vessels of coconut and so on. Bone refers to conches and so on. As for horn: by a paste of white mustard seeds. This is the meaning.

And further (┼Ъaс╣Еkha 16.11тАУ12ab):[^FNB000451]

тБ╕┬╣Sprinkling is the method of purification for resins, molasses, salts, safflower flowers, wool and cotton: so says Lord Yama.

Resins refer to asafoetida and so on.

Broo

Manu (5.118тАУ119, 122):[^FNB000452]

тБ╕┬▓Many clothes or much grain is purified by sprinkling with water; a small amount with sprinkling just a little water. тБ╕┬│Skins and bamboo items are purified like clothes, while the purification of green leafy vegetables, roots and fruits is said to be like that of grain. тБ╕тБ┤Grass, wood and straw is also cleansed by sprinkling, while the house is cleansed by sweeping and smearing and clay items by reheating.

Bamboo items refer to those made of split bamboo, reeds or leaves. Sweeping means removing dust. [тАж]

And further (Manu 5.126):[^FNB000453]

тБ╕тБ╡One should apply mud and water onto an item smeared with something impure until the stain and the smell is gone. This applies to the cleansing of all types of items.

Bс╣Ыhaspati (тАУ):[^FNB000454]

тБ╕тБ╢The purification of clothes, bamboos, skins and so on is done through sprinkling. To clean something very contaminated, that part should be cut off and discarded.

That part: only that part which has become very contaminated. тАЬNot the rest of itтАЭ is the implied meaning.

Viс╣гс╣Зu (тАУ):

тБ╕тБ╖Clay, leaves, grass and wood that have been touched by a dog, bone, a C─Бс╣Зс╕Нala or by a crow is purified by the shine of the moon and the sun and by the wind.

Broo

Baudh─Бyana (1.5.62):[^FNB000455]

тБ╕тБ╕A seat, bed, vehicle, boat, grass and a path are purified by wind and sun; so also surfaces covered with burned bricks.

Wind and sun means by the rays of the sun accompanied by the wind. The other reading is clear.[^FNB000456]

Grains and so on

Baudh─Бyana (тАУ):

тБ╕тБ╣Rice, green leafy vegetables, roots and fruits: by sprinkling with water or by removing the contaminated part, and by husking.

┼Ъaс╣Еkha (тАУ):

тБ╣тБ░Ghee and oil, by boiling; milk, by overflowing. Vessels should be overflowed by water, so also green leafy vegetables and fruits.

Boiling means cooking. The author else describes overflowing. The vessels of various liquids should be made to overflow or be plunged into water. Also, if ghee and similar substances cannot be boiled, it should be understood that they can be purified by overflowing them with the same substance.[^FNB000457]

Broo

In the Brahma Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000458]

тБ╣┬╣Large amounts of liquids should be overflowed with water; so also grains, rice, green leafy vegetables, roots and fruits. One should discard the contaminated part and then have them overflowed with water.

One should discard the contaminated part refers to cases of major pollution.

Bс╣Ыhaspati (тАУ):[^FNB000459]

тБ╣┬▓Ghee and oils should be purified by heating; milk, by overflowing. Condensed milk and thick sour milk are purified by removing the part in question. So also with coagulated ghee, but melted ghee by boiling.

The part in question means as much as has been contaminated. This also refers to things without a particular form.

And elsewhere:[^FNB000460]

тБ╣┬│When there is a fault of location, one should pour a liquid from that container to another. тБ╣тБ┤Ghee, P─Бyasa, milk, sugarcane juice, molasses, sour milk and honey are never polluted by staying in the vessel of a ┼Ъ┼лdra.

In verse93 here, the author gives specifics about the source vessel. [тАж] The same is said by Yama:[^FNB000461] тАЬRaw meat, ghee, honey and fruit juices are polluted when in the vessel of a Mleccha, but when taken out, they are known to be pure.тАЭ And elsewhere: тАЬAll sources elsewhere are pure.тАЭ

Furthermore, Manu (5.143):

тБ╣тБ╡A person who is somehow touched by food leavings while carrying an item becomes clean by ─Аcamana without putting down that item.

Broo

тБ╣тБ╢Also other rules for purification of items should be learnt from the Smс╣Ыtis and treatises, if they apply to Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas. Enough with all these words!

According to Sad─Бc─Бra, food should be understood as an exception to becomes clean. Concerning food, ─Аpastambha says (9.34cdтАУ35): тАЬIf one somehow passes stool or urine while carrying an item, one should put the food down on the ground and bathe in the proper way. When one then touches the cooked food, it becomes clean by this connection.тАЭ And Bс╣Ыhaspati (тАУ):[^FNB000462] тАЬFirst one should do purification, then sprinkle the feet. After one has sipped water, one should touch what one had brought and it will become pure.тАЭ

Even though these kinds of pollution do not befall the items of the Lord, still these kinds of purification have been given as they apply to offerings of all of these different items for the sake of the Lord, or since all these types of pollution are possible through mistakes or carelessness. This is the drift. If they apply to Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas, then they should be learnt from the Smс╣Ыtis and treatises. As it is said, тАЬAt a pilgrimage, a wedding, a festival, a battle, when the country is beset with calamity or when the city or village is on fire, touching or not touching causes no pollutionтАЭ,[^FNB000463] тАЬOne should not consider purity in a pasture, in a cookery, at an oil press, a sugarcane press or among women, children or the sickтАЭ,[^FNB000464] and so on. Therefore, enough with all these words! There is no need for them, as there is the fear of making the book too extensive. This is the meaning.

Picking Flowers, Tulas─л and so on for the Sake of Worship

тБ╣тБ╖Now, having bowed to great Viс╣гс╣Зu, the Vaiс╣гс╣Зava should pray for his permission and then collect Tulas─л, flowers and so on, as has been indicated.

And so on refers to items such as leaves and buds. As has been indicated means taking care to avoid forbidden items and so on.

Rules for Bathing at Home

┬╣тБ░тБ░One who wishes to bathe at home should sprinkle water on hands and feet, do ─Аcamana, control the breathing, do Ny─Бsa and remember Hari.

Control the breathing means to do Pr─Бс╣З─Бy─Бma.

┬╣тБ░┬╣Then, remembering sacred rivers such as the Ganges, the practitioner should invoke all the T─лrthas into a pot filled with water mixed with Tulas─л.

And this is the mantra of invocation:[^FNB000468]

┬╣тБ░┬▓Ganges! Yamun─Б! God─Бvar─л! Sarasvat─л! Narmad─Б! Sindhu! K─Бver─л! Please enter this water.

┬╣тБ░┬│Alternatively, the wise one should invoke only the Ganges, the embodiment of all T─лrthas, into a vessel of water, using her twelve names.

And they are said to be:[^FNB000469]

┬╣тБ░тБ┤Nalin─л (Lotus), Nandin─л (Gladdening), S─лt─Б (Furrow), M─Бlin─л (Garlanded), Mah─Бpag─Б (Great river), Viс╣гс╣Зup─Бd─Бrghyasambh┼лt─Б (Born of the

armlets and a splendid golden crown, this God, all of whose limbs are beautiful and who is decorated with all kinds of ornaments! ┬╣┬╣┬▓One should meditate on the flow from his lotus foot falling down onto oneтАЩs head and entering oneтАЩs body through the Brahmarandhra, thereby completely cleansing all the dirt of the inner body. ┬╣┬╣┬│Immediately the practitioner becomes spotless like a crystal. This best bathing is known to be a thousand times better than a mantra bath.

┬╣┬╣тБ┤Because of statements such as тАЬO son, a man who utters тАШN─Бr─Бyaс╣ЗaтАЩ once тАжтАЭ (3.34) one should remember the great Lord and recite his name at the time of bathing.

[тАж] Such as refers to the indications of other statements as well, for example тАЬOne should meditate on Lord N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa тАжтАЭ (3.119). On their basis one should recite his, N─Бr─Бyaс╣ЗaтАЩs, name.

As also in the K┼лrma Pur─Бс╣Зa (2.18.62):[^FNB000473]

┬╣┬╣тБ╡Since water has come from N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa and since it is his abode (ayana), the intelligent one should remember Lord N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa at the time of bathing.

┬╣┬╣тБ╢Even though healthy, one should bathe also with warm water, with myrobalan, sesamum seeds and oil, but one should avoid forbidden days.

One should use not only cold water but warm water too, and this applies not only to those who are unwell. Healthy means that one has no illness or the like. Yama (тАУ) says that those who are ill should always bathe with warm water: тАЬThat which has been heated by the rays of the sun or again cleansed by fire should not be used for bathing, but boiled water is recommended for the bathing of the sick.тАЭ The forbidden days are given below (4.121тАУ122).

Bathing with Warm Water

In the с╣вaс╣нtriс╣Г┼Ыanmata:

┬╣┬╣тБ╖Water is naturally purifying and especially so in connection with fire. The saints therefore praise bathing with warm water.

Broo

And Yama (тАУ):

┬╣┬╣тБ╕Water is by itself always clean, especially so when heated by fire. Therefore, warm water is always known to be purifying.

And when it is said by ┼Ъaс╣Еkha (8.10):

┬╣┬╣тБ╣It should be known that when one bathes with water heated by fire or the sun, oneтАЩs body is cleaned but one does not get the fruit of bathing.

that refers to optional or occasional rituals. Therefore, it is said by Garga (тАУ):

┬╣┬▓тБ░In the case of occasional and optional bathing, one should use cold water, but in the case of mandatory and spontaneous bathing, one should do as one likes.

The meaning is that in the case of both mandatory or spontaneous, that is, non-regulated bathing, one may use cold or warm water according to oneтАЩs liking. Spontaneous bathing can also refer to bathing for oneтАЩs pleasure.

The Forbidden Days

In this connection, Yama says (тАУ):

┬╣┬▓┬╣At the birth of a son, when the sun enters a new sign, at a solar or lunar eclipse or when one has touched something untouchable, one should not bathe with warm water.

The elder Manu:

┬╣┬▓┬▓One who bathes with warm water at the full moon or new moon here incurs the sin of killing a cow, without a doubt.

Bathing with Myrobalan[^FNB000474]

In this connection, M─Бrkaс╣Зс╕Нeya says (тАУ):[^FNB000475]

┬╣┬▓┬│Viс╣гс╣Зu is pleased by myrobalan, especially on Ek─Бda┼Ы─л. A man who desires glory should always bathe with myrobalan. ┬╣┬▓тБ┤On Saptam─л, one should not touch oil, wear blue clothes, bathe with myrobalan or quarrel.

Bhс╣Ыgu (тАУ):[^FNB000476]

┬╣┬▓тБ╡On the new moon day, on с╣вaс╣гс╣нh─л, Saptam─л, Navam─л, Trayoda┼Ы─л, when the sun enters a new sign and on Saturday one should avoid bathing with myrobalan.

Y─Бj├▒avalkya (тАУ):[^FNB000477]

┬╣┬▓тБ╢One who bathes with the myrobalan fruit on the new moon day, Saptam─л or Navam─л loses his splendour, longevity, riches and sons.

Bathing with Sesame

In this connection, Bс╣Ыhaspati says (тАУ):

┬╣┬▓тБ╖Sage Vy─Бsa also said that one should always bathe with sesame.

In the с╣вaс╣нtriс╣Г┼Ыanmata:

┬╣┬▓тБ╕Also, one who desires riches, sons and wives should not touch that which has touched sesame on Saptam─л, the new moon day, when the sun enters a new sign or at an eclipse.

Broo

Bathing with Oil

In the same book:

┬╣┬▓тБ╣Oil is not vivifying on с╣вaс╣гс╣нh─л or during the four moon festivals.

Yogiy─Бj├▒avalkya (тАУ):

┬╣┬│тБ░Four things are destroyed for that fool who bathes on Da┼Ыam─л without touching oil: his longevity, understanding, renown and wealth.

On Da┼Ыam─л without touching oil establishes the necessity of bathing with oil at that time.

┬╣┬│┬╣These four abandon one who by mistake anoints himself with oil on the first, the sixth, the new moon day or on an empty day.[^FNB000478]

These four: longevity and so on as mentioned above (4.130).

┬╣┬│┬▓One should avoid touching oil on the sixth, seventh, twelfth, fourteenth and fifteenth day and when the sun enters a new sign.[^FNB000479]

And elsewhere:

┬╣┬│┬│Especially on the first, seventh, eighth, ninth, fourteenth day or during the new moon on should not touch oil.[^FNB000480]

Especially: this word indicates the necessity to give up oil on the first day and so on.

Moreover:

┬╣┬│тБ┤Whether for bathing or not, the oil from roasted sesame seeds does not pollute.[^FNB000481]

In this verse, the author gives an exception to what has been stated above: the oil from roasted sesame seeds never carries any fault.

And moreover, in the Atri Smс╣Ыti (Atri Saс╣Гhit─Б 187ab, 188ab):

┬╣┬│тБ╡A Br─Бhmaс╣Зa who passes urine or stool while anointed with oil or ghee is purified by eating the five products of the cow after fasting for a day and a night.

Incidentally, the author states with this verse that one should not pass urine or stool after anointing oneтАЩs limbs with oil. [тАж] But in another reading, one should carefully avoid touching an untouchable in such a situation. This is the implied meaning.[^FNB000482]

┬╣┬│тБ╢Then, sufficiently stretching out oneтАЩs limbs, one should bathe and in the proper way do Aghamarс╣гaс╣Зa with a handful of water close to the nose. ┬╣┬│тБ╖Then, having sprinkled oneself with the foot-water of the preceptor and so on as above, one should anoint oneself with water from a conch, mixed with Tulas─л.

The Greatness of Anointing with Tulas─л Water

In the Garuс╕Нa Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000483]

┬╣┬│тБ╕O twice-born one! That Vaiс╣гс╣Зava who at the time of anointing rubs himself with Tulas─л immediately gets a body made up of all the T─лrthas. ┬╣┬│тБ╣Even were one the killer of a Br─Бhmaс╣Зa, by bathing with Tulas─л water particularly on Ek─Бda┼Ы─л one is freed from all sins. ┬╣тБ┤тБ░One who day after day bathes after anointing his limbs with mud from its roots attains the fruit of the Avabhс╣Ыta bath after ten horse sacrifices. ┬╣тБ┤┬╣Water mixed with Tulas─л leaves is known as equal to the Ganges. it on his head carries J─Бhnav─л herself. ┬╣тБ┤┬▓One who takes water mixed with Tulas─л leaves on his head without a doubt attains the result of bathing at all T─лrthas.

Rules for Wearing Clothes

In this connection, Atri (тАУ):[^FNB000484]

┬╣тБ┤тБ╢One should avoid clothes and undergarments that are unwashed, washed by a washerman, washed on an earlier day, are stained or dirty. One should never dress in half of a garment.

Bhс╣Ыgu (тАУ):[^FNB000485]

┬╣тБ┤тБ╖Wearing dirty clothes is being naked; wearing half a garment is being naked; wearing a cloth folded twice is being naked and wearing a red garment is being naked.

Or naked means clothed in the directions alone (digambara), a type of Jain.

┬╣тБ┤тБ╕Wearing stitched clothes is being naked, wearing a greasy garment is being naked; tucking in twice,[^FNB000486] not wearing an upper cloth and being without garments is being naked. ┬╣тБ┤тБ╣One should not even think about performing ┼Ъrauta or Sm─Бrta rites naked. One who by mistake does so goes down; that ritual will be a demonic one. ┬╣тБ╡тБ░At recitations, fire sacrifices, fasts, ┼Ъr─Бddhas and so on one should wear clean clothing, be ornamented, clean, silent and restrain oneтАЩs senses.

Gobhila (тАУ):[^FNB000487]

┬╣тБ╡┬╣Wearing one garment one should not eat nor worship the gods.

In the Trailokyasammohana Pa├▒car─Бtra:[^FNB000488]

┬╣тБ╡┬▓One should always wear white clothes and avoid red ones.

Aс╣Еgiras (44cdтАУ45ab):

┬╣тБ╡┬│That of the thousand-haired ones is cleaned by the air, fire and the rays of the sun and the moon. Wool is not polluted even when touched by semen or a corpse.

That of the thousand or innumerable haired ones means blankets and so on made of their wool. Wool refers to blankets and so on made of sheep hair.[^FNB000489]

fathers is said to be imperishable, like that at a ┼Ъr─Бddha in Gay─Б. ┬╣тБ╡тБ╡O king, never perform rituals to the gods wearing stitched clothes, never wear burned or cut clothes or those of a stranger. ┬╣тБ╡тБ╢Unwashed clothes are said to be the same as the stool of a crow; clothes that have been brought from the washerman are also unclean. ┬╣тБ╡тБ╖One should further avoid clothes that have been touched by the buttocks, that is, used while passing stool or urine or having intercourse.[^FNB000491] ┬╣тБ╡тБ╕Best of kings! Broo

It was said (161) that after getting dressed, one should perform ─Аcamana sitting on a seat. This seat is described in verses162тАУ165.

┬╣тБ╢┬│The wise one should always avoid seats made of cow dung and mud, Arka, Pal─Б┼Ыa or Pippala wood, that are broken or studded with iron.

Rules for the Seat[^FNB000494]

In the same book:[^FNB000495]

┬╣тБ╢тБ┤One should not give charity, do ─Аcamana, perform sacrifices, eat, worship the gods, do oneтАЩs Vedic reading or offer libations while squatting. ┬╣тБ╢тБ╡Keeping the feet on the seat or tying up the knees or shanks is called squatting.

┬╣тБ╢тБ╢Then, keeping oneтАЩs foot on the ground, one should sit down, perform ─Аcamana with a Ku┼Ыa ring and then draw the vertical marks and so on with Gop─лcandana or similar substances.

[тАж] Even though it is proper to do ─Аcamana after drawing the vertical marks, it is still written here, following the tradition of the saints, that ─Аcamana comes first when occasioned by special cases such as drawing Tilakas for the sake of worship. [тАж]

┬╣тБ╢тБ╖In this connection, one should first wipe all of oneтАЩs limbs with the unction from the lotus feet of the Lord and with flowers offered to him.

[тАж]

This has been said by the blessed Lord in the Brahma Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000496]

┬╣тБ╢тБ╕O lotus-seated one! To attain the greatest purity, one should always wear the sandalwood paste that has touched the ┼Ъ─Бlagr─Бma stone on all oneтАЩs limbs.

┬╣тБ╢тБ╣Then, with the twelve names beginning with Ke┼Ыava, the Vaiс╣гс╣Зava should in the proper way make the twelve vertical marks on the body.

One should make the twelve vertical marks on twelve parts of the body, beginning with the forehead, one after the other, using the twelve names beginning with Ke┼Ыava, as explained in the M┼лrtipa├▒jara Ny─Бsa.[^FNB000497] By using the word Vaiс╣гс╣Зava, the author indicates that is particularly necessary for the Vaiс╣гс╣Зava.

тАЬLet it be done in the proper wayтАЭ: here is the rule. Following the M┼лrtipa├▒jara Ny─Бsa, one should place the twelve names beginning with Ke┼Ыava, prefixed with

Oс╣В, together with the twelve ─Аdityas and twelve vowels beginning with A with a Bindu added. In this connection, some place Ke┼Ыava and so on together with the twelve ┼Ъaktis, beginning with K─лrti. These are the twelve ─Аdityas: Dh─Бtс╣Ы, ─Аryaman, Mitra, Varuс╣Зa, Aс╣Г┼Ыu, Bhaga, Vivasv─Бn, Indra, P┼лс╣гan, Parjanya, Tvaс╣гс╣нс╣Ы and Viс╣гс╣Зu. And this is the procedure:

Oс╣В Aс╣В DH─АTс╣ЪSAHIT─АYA KE┼ЪAV─АYA K─кRTYAI NAMAс╕д on the forehead, and so on.[^FNB000498]

Furthermore, the various shapes of the vertical mark on the forehead, such as that of a rosary, will be explained below (4.190). Some describe the vertical marks on the other parts of the body as well as having the shape of the flame of a lamp, and some, following the statement in the Uttarakhaс╣Зс╕Нa of the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (6.225.50ab) that тАЬthe marks on the arms and the chest should be eight digits longтАЭ, hold that the marks on the arms and the chest should measure eight digits while the others should measure four digits.

Some further wish to keep the middle empty (Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa 6.225.23). There are therefore various rules. Here also one should follow the practice of oneтАЩs own tradition; that is the reason why the author writes below (4.175) тАЬfollowing tradition.тАЭ

The Rules for the Twelve Tilakas

In the Uttarakhaс╣Зс╕Нa of the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (6.225.45тАУ47ab):[^FNB000499]

┬╣тБ╖тБ░One should meditate on Ke┼Ыava on the forehead, N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa on the belly, M─Бdhava on the chest, Govinda in the cavity of the throat, ┬╣тБ╖┬╣Viс╣гс╣Зu on the right side, Madhus┼лdana on the arm, Trivikrama on the shoulder, V─Бmana on the left side, ┬╣тБ╖┬▓┼Ъr─лdhara on the left arm and Hс╣Ыс╣г─лke┼Ыa on the shoulder. One should place Padman─Бbha on the upper back and D─Бmodara on the lower back. ┬╣тБ╖┬│Saying тАЬV─БsudevaтАЭ, one should wipe the water for washing on the head.

In verses170тАУ172, the author shows how to divide these names among the parts of the body. Meditate on means place. Trivikrama on the right shoulder and Hс╣Ыс╣г─лke┼Ыa on the left shoulder. After saying that one should place all twelve, beginning with Ke┼Ыava and ending with D─Бmodara, the author states that one should place blessed V─Бsudeva on the head in verse173. V─Бsudeva means

V─АSUDEV─АYA NAMAс╕д, and this should be placed with all the vowels. And some place the twelve-syllable mantra on the head. Here also one should have recourse to the conduct of the tradition of saints. This is the drift.

And further (6.225.54):

┬╣тБ╖тБ┤The vertical mark on the forehead is known as the first of them all. The rule is that one should mark them one after the other, starting with the forehead.

┬╣тБ╖тБ╡In this way one should do the Ny─Бsa following tradition. One should also place the Crown mantra on the head to attain all of oneтАЩs desires.

The phrase following tradition should be supplied everywhere below as well.

The Crown Mantra[^FNB000500]

┬╣тБ╖тБ╢

Oс╣В! I bow to him who is glowing like a thousand suns, shining through his own light, accompanied as he is by ┼Ъr─л and Bh┼лmi, whose chest is marked with the ┼Ъr─лvatsa, who wears yellow garments, the disc, conch, club and lotus, Makara-shaped earrings, bracelets, necklaces and a blessed crown.

The Mandatoriness of the Vertical Marks

In the words of the Lord in the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000501]

┬╣тБ╖тБ╖O four-faced one, to please me, to look good or for protection, my composed devotee should always wear the vertical mark that takes away all fear: at the time of worshipping me, at night and in the morning.

The phrase should always wear establishes the mandatoriness.

In the words of N─Бrada in the same book:[^FNB000502]

┬╣тБ╖тБ╕Sacrifice, charity, penance, fire ceremonies, Vedic study, libations to the forefathersтАФeverything becomes worthless when done without the vertical mark.

In the Uttarakhaс╣Зс╕Нa of the same book (6.225.11, 13):

┬╣тБ╖тБ╣Whatever someone does without the vertical marksтАФrites for oneself or for othersтАФall of that will without a doubt be fruitless. ┬╣тБ╕тБ░One who regularly performs the Sandhy─Б- or other rites without the vertical marks makes them all demonic and will go to hell.

Now, in these verses, the author shows the heaps of offences caused by their neglect. [тАж]

Broo

┬▓тБ░┬▓A man who dies anywhere, but who wears the vertical mark mounts a celestial chariot and is honoured in my world, even were he a dog-eater. ┬▓тБ░┬│I rescue from hell twenty generations of the family of one in whose house a man who wears the vertical mark partakes of food.

[тАж]

Rules for Drawing the Vertical Mark

In the Brahm─Бс╣Зс╕Нa Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000509]

┬▓тБ░тБ┤Fortunate one! One who carefully makes the vertical mark looking in a mirror or in water reaches the highest destination. ┬▓тБ░тБ╡The one measuring ten digits is said to be the very best of best, the one measuring nine digits is middling and then comes the one measuring eight digits.[^FNB000510] ┬▓тБ░тБ╢One should make the mark differentiating the fingers, but one should not touch with the nails.

Since the vertical mark on the forehead is the main one, he gives the rules for creating that vertical mark in these verses. Then comes means the inferior.

In the Uttarakhaс╣Зс╕Нa of the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (6.225.21, 40тАУ43):[^FNB000511]

┬▓тБ░тБ╖The fortunate, exclusive devotees, who delight in benefitting all, make a mark like the foot of Hari with an intermediate space. ┬▓тБ░тБ╕They say that a dark one brings peace; a red one, subjection; a yellow one, fortune and a beautiful white one, liberation. ┬▓тБ░тБ╣A round, horizontal, undivided, short, longer, thin, bent or ugly mark, with its top bound together, root divided or out of place; ┬▓┬╣тБ░that is disagreeable, rough, sticking, not made with the fingers, smelly or to the leftтАФthey say such a mark is offensive.

┬▓┬╣┬╣Beginning from the root of the nose and ending at the brow one should draw with mud. The third part of the nose are called the тАЬroot of the nose.тАЭ ┬▓┬╣┬▓Beginning from between the eyebrows one should make an intermediate space.

With an intermediate space means empty in middle. In this way, the author describes the form of HariтАЩs foot. In another reading, the word -tatam [instead of -─Бkс╣Ыtam, form] means тАЬspreadтАЭ. Out of place means fallen from its position. Disagreeable means dirty. Sticking means with the lines touching each other. The other reading is easy.[^FNB000512] Smelly means having a bad odour. To the left means made with the left hand. Third part means the third portion. This can also be seen from observing Sad─Бc─Бra.

The Mandatoriness of the Empty Middle Portion of the Vertical Mark

In the same book (6.255.26тАУ27, 24cd):

┬▓┬╣┬│That lowest of the twice-born who makes a vertical mark without the intermediate space drives away the Viс╣гс╣Зu and Lakс╣гm─л who stay there. ┬▓┬╣тБ┤Those lowest of the twice-born who make an undivided vertical mark always have the footprint of a dog on their foreheads, without a doubt. ┬▓┬╣тБ╡Therefore, beautiful one, both Br─Бhmaс╣Зas and women should always wear a beautiful, straight and divided vertical mark.

Drives away means banishes. By stating this great fault, the mandatoriness [of the empty middle space] is explained. Similar places below should be taken in the same way.

Broo

Regularly draws the vertical mark

Will always have the fruit of his deeds a million times over.

┬▓┬│┬╣Even without rituals, without mantras,

Without faith and disregarding timeтАФ

One who places Gopicandana on the forehead

Will always attain an imperishable reward for his work.

Gopicandana with a short i is an archaic irregularity. Even should be connected with the following lines. Even if the work is lacking in ritual and so on, nevertheless, one who places Gop─лcandana on the forehead will by making this vertical mark attain its eternal fruit. This is the meaning.

┬▓┬│тБ╢O bird, by the mercy of Hari,

the planets do not disturb, nor R─Бkс╣гasas,

nor Yakс╣гas, Pi┼Ы─Бcas, Uragas, Bh┼лtas or D─Бnavas,

the one on whose forehead Gop─лcandana resides.

[тАж]

By Gautama in the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000520]

┬▓┬│тБ╖Ambar─лс╣гa! In order to remove a great sin, look at those who regularly make a mark on their foreheads with Gop─лcandana.

And by Yama in the K─Б┼Ы─лkhaс╣Зс╕Нa (4.7.108):

┬▓┬│тБ╕Listen messengers! Like burning coal you should carefully avoid that person whose forehead is marked with Gop─лcandana.

[тАж]

┬▓┬│тБ╣Now, on top of that, Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas should in the same place make a delightful vertical mark with mud from the root of the blessed Tulas─л.

The Greatness of Marks Made with Mud from the Roots of Tulas─л

In connection with clay from the roots of Tulas─л in the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000521]

┬▓тБ┤тБ░Those men who wear a mark made with this clay have constructed a proof of their proceeding towards liberation.

From the context, this clay means the clay from the roots of Tulas─л. [тАж]

In a discussion between Brahm─Б and N─Бrada in the Greatness of K─Бrttika in the same book (2.4.6.33):[^FNB000522]

┬▓тБ┤┬╣N─Бrada! Even the body of one on whose forehead can be seen a mark made of Tulas─л clay, cannot be touched by sin as it is committed.

[тАж]. Even as it is committed sin cannot touch even the body of the one committing it, let alone his mind and so on. This is the meaning.

And in the Garuс╕Нa Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000523]

┬▓тБ┤┬▓From the sight of one who day after day makes a mark with Tulas─л clay, the sin that men commit in a year disappears.

┬▓тБ┤┬│On top of this should be smeared the remnants of the Lord, for wearing marks in exactly this way is known as the threefold Tilaka. ┬▓тБ┤тБ┤Then, to please Hari, one should wear the Mudr─Бs of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa: the marks of Matsya, K┼лrma and so on, and the disc and the other weapons.

The Mandatoriness of Wearing the Mudr─Бs

In the Smс╣Ыti:[^FNB000524]

┬▓тБ┤тБ╡One should always worship Hari while marked with the conch and the disc on the shoulders, for otherwise there will not be any worship.

In the ─Аditya Pur─Бс╣Зa:

┬▓тБ┤тБ╢A king should place that lowest of Br─Бhmaс╣Зas who is bereft of the conch, the disc and the vertical mark on an ass and banish him from his kingdom.

┬▓тБ┤тБ╖It is said that those who are clean are eligible for all rituals, and it should be known that by wearing my weapons, one becomes clean.

In the Uttarakhaс╣Зс╕Нa of the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (6.253.120cdтАУ121ab):

┬▓тБ┤тБ╣That great one who, wearing the vertical mark and made disc,

meditates on supreme Viс╣гс╣Зu,

the most supreme, the one greater than the greatтАж

And in the Atharva Veda:

may we be fortunate in this world!

Those who are marked will go to

that supreme abode of Viс╣гс╣Зu.[^FNB000526]

┬▓тБ╡┬╣To B─Бс╣гkala[^FNB000527] goes the merit accumulated over twelve years for one who does not offer respect when seeing one marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons.

[тАж] What can be said about the greatness of wearing the Mudr─Бs? With this verse, the author writes that it follows from the statement of the Brahma Pur─Бс╣Зa that even showing respect to people who wear them is mandatory.

The Greatness of Wearing the Mudr─Бs

In a discussion between Sanatkum─Бra and M─Бrkaс╣Зс╕Нeya in the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬▓тБ╡┬▓Greatest of Br─Бhmaс╣Зas! That devotee of Viс╣гс╣Зu who is marked with the conch, disc and so, goes to the world of Viс╣гс╣Зu, free from the fire of destruction.

Elsewhere in the same book (2.5.3.30тАУ34):[^FNB000528]

┬▓тБ╡┬│What can Yama do with one whose body is always marked with the weapons of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa, even had he committed millions of sins? ┬▓тБ╡тБ┤The merit said to accrue from living at ┼Ъaс╣Еkhoddhara[^FNB000529] for millions of years accrues to the one who daily draws the conch on his right arm. ┬▓тБ╡тБ╡The merit of always seeing Puс╣Зс╕Нar─лk─Бkс╣гa at Puс╣гkara comes to him who draws the lotus above the conch. ┬▓тБ╡тБ╢To one on whose left arm one can see the club in the age of Kali, Gad─Бdhara every day gives the merit of Gay─Б. ┬▓тБ╡тБ╖And that merit which is described to come from being in the proximity of Cakrasv─Бmin in ─Аnandapura, that comes when seeing Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa when marked with the disc below the club.[^FNB000530]

In the words of the Lord:[^FNB000531]

^(258тАУ259)Best of the thirty gods! You should know that I enter the body of that man who, moreover, in the age of Kali collects mud from my city and makes the signs of the fish, the tortoise and so on. One who desires welfare should not differentiate between him and me. ┬▓тБ╢тБ░One on whose body can be seen the signs of my descents should be not known as a mortal by mortals: he indeed is my body.

[тАж] My body means that he is a descent of me.

┬▓тБ╢┬╣For one who in the age of Kali draws my weapons on his body, sin takes the form of virtue. ┬▓тБ╢┬▓And I send down my own brilliance into the body of one who is marked with both the signs, that of the fish and that of the tortoise.

the conch, the lotus, the club and the disc,

one ever increases oneтАЩs fortune

and destroys sins accumulated over a hundred births.

[тАж] That the word sin is an attribute to a hundred births even though it is part of a separate compound is an archaic irregularity.

In the same book, in a discussion between Brahm─Б and N─Бrada:[^FNB000532]

┬▓тБ╢тБ┤The armour made by Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons cannot be pierced by gods of demons; it is invisible to all living beings, for enemies and even R─Бkс╣гasas. ┬▓тБ╢тБ╡Lakс╣гm─л, Sarasvat─л, Durg─Б and S─Бvitr─л, beloved of Hari,[^FNB000533] all eternally stay in the body of one who has marked his form with the conch. ┬▓тБ╢тБ╢The Ganges, Gay─Б, Kurukс╣гetra, Pray─Бga, Puс╣гkara and other pilgrimage sites always remain with one who has marked his body with the lotus. ┬▓тБ╢тБ╖Mischievous one, when one has marked his left arm with the Kaumodak─л club, one can see the confluence of the Ganges and the ocean there every day. ┬▓тБ╢тБ╕If the disc resides underneath the club on the left arm then the three worlds of moving and unmoving creatures, together with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, ┬▓тБ╢тБ╣the three fires, the three gods and the three steps of Viс╣гс╣Зu will always reside there, in him on whose body Sudar┼Ыana dwells.

┬▓тБ╖тБ░One who wears the Mudr─Б of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa, the mark of Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons on the arm, becomes eligible for the upper worlds; he should be known as the master of the thirty gods. ┬▓тБ╖┬╣All the mandatory, occasional or optional rituals for the gods or the ancestors of one who is marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs Mudr─Бs, become imperishable, day after day. ┬▓тБ╖┬▓One who wears the metallic Mudr─Б, decorated with the eight syllables, on his arm will never be plagued by the planets, the stars or the signs.

In a statement of Sanatkum─Бra in the Var─Бha Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000535]

┬▓тБ╖┬│What is the point of going to T─лrthas such as Pray─Бga when the body has been marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons through Gop─лcandana mud? ┬▓тБ╖тБ┤When he sees someoneтАЩs body marked with the signs of the conch and so on, at that very time the master of the worlds happily takes away his sin. ┬▓тБ╖тБ╡And that body on which day and night, day after day, the conch, disc, club and lotus are drawn, is Acyuta himself.

To use the middle voice for seen (prapa┼Ыyeta) and is (bhavate) are archaic irregularities.

┬▓тБ╖тБ╢One who joins himself to N─Бr─Бyaс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons in the age of Kali performs good deeds equal to Mount Meru! ┬▓тБ╖тБ╖O Br─Бhmaс╣Зa! [тАж] The sins of oneself or of others are burned up. The meaning is that they are destroyed by themselves.

^(279тАУ280)Mischievous one, that Bh─Бgavata devotee who especially in the age of Kali wears a Mudr─Б which is decorated with Viс╣гс╣ЗuтАЩs name, the eight syllables and the weapons of the conch and so on, and which is made of gold or silver, should be known as equal to Prahl─Бda and in no other way.

┬▓тБ╕┬╣The food that a Br─Бhmaс╣Зa whose body is marked with the conch eats in anyoneтАЩs house is eaten by Ke┼Ыava himself together with the ancestors. ┬▓тБ╕┬▓And N─Бrada, if one who is marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons dies [even] at a crematorium, he attains the destination ordained for dying at Pray─Бga. ┬▓тБ╕┬│The gods led by Indra take shelter of one whose body is always adorned with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons in the age of Kali!

If: if he should happen to die at a crematorium. This is the meaning. Using the neuter for the [masculine] word vigraha is an archaic irregularity.

┬▓тБ╕тБ┤Ke┼Ыava constantly takes away thousands of offences from that man who worships Hari marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons. ┬▓тБ╕тБ╡There is no Vaiс╣гс╣Зava equal to him who makes a wooden stamp marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons and then marks himself. ┬▓тБ╕тБ╢That man who is marked with Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons cannot be touched by the deceitful doings of heretics, fallen people, vagrants or the sinful prattle of the deniers.

┬▓тБ╕тБ╖One who has a metallic Mudr─Б with the eight syllables and the conch, lotus and so on is worshipped by both gods and demons.

┬▓тБ╕тБ╕Previously, in the Kс╣Ыta age, Prahl─Бda wore the Mudr─Бs of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa, as did Vibh─лс╣гaс╣Зa, Bali, Dhruva and ┼Ъuka. ┬▓тБ╕тБ╣Mischievous one, M─Бndh─Бtс╣Ыс╣З, Ambar─лс╣гa, M─Бrkaс╣Зс╕Нa and other Br─Бhmaс╣Зas made on their bodies with the weapons, the signs of the conch and so on. And further:[^FNB000542]

┬▓тБ╣┬│If one wears the N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa Mudr─Б, marked with the conch and so on, on oneтАЩs body and marks all the limbs with N─Бr─Бyaс╣ЗaтАЩs weapons, no sins can enter. This is the armour of Viс╣гс╣Зu.

And elsewhere:[^FNB000543]

┬▓тБ╣тБ┤In the age of Kali, the twice-born attain the power to curse and bless in the world of mortals through these signs of the Lord.

Rules for Wearing the Mudr─Бs

┬▓тБ╣тБ╡One should wear the disc on the right arm, the conch on the left or right, the club on the left and underneath the club another disc. ┬▓тБ╣тБ╢On top of the conch one should wear the lotus and another lotus on the right, the sword on the chest and bow and arrow on the head. ┬▓тБ╣тБ╖In this way, a Vaiс╣гс╣Зava should wear the five weapons; also, Matsya on the right arm and K┼лrma on the left.

One should wear the conch on the right arm. Even though statements such as the one beginning with тАЬA Br─Бhmaс╣Зa should wear Sudar┼Ыana on the right arm тАжтАЭ (4.298) say that one should wear the conch on the left arm, nevertheless, following statements such as the one beginning with тАЬThe merit said to accrue from living at ┼Ъaс╣Еkhoddhara тАжтАЭ (4.254), the author states again the one can wear the conch on the right as well. One should wear the sword on the chest and bow and arrow on the head. Following a statement of the Var─Бha Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ), the procedure for wearing branded Mudr─Бs will be given below (15.103): тАЬOne should wear the club on the forehead, bow and arrow on the head, the Nandaka sword in the middle of the chest and conch and disc on the arms.тАЭ[^FNB000544] Nevertheless, it will be explicitly said below (4.299) that following oneтАЩs own inclination, all can be worn everywhere. This is the drift. The five weapons are the disc, conch, club, sword and bow.

It is also said:[^FNB000545]

┬▓тБ╣тБ╕A Br─Бhmaс╣Зa should wear Sudar┼Ыana, Matsya and the lotus on the right arm; and on the other, the conch, K┼лrma and the club.

[тАж]

┬▓тБ╣тБ╣Following the custom of the traditionтАЩs stalwarts and according to oneтАЩs own inclination, the marks of the conch and so on can be worn on all limbs.[^FNB000546] ┬│тБ░тБ░According to oneтАЩs devotion, one can also wear the marks of oneтАЩs own chosen divinity. Some also wear the disc and conch combined with each other.[^FNB000547]

The marks refer to the flute and so on. Wearing other marks of the Lord than the five weapons is forbidden in the Uttarakhaс╣Зda of the Padma Pur─Бс╣Зa (6.224.51): тАЬA Br─Бhmaс╣Зa should not brand the body with anything else than the signs of Hari: the conch, disc, club, lotus and bowтАЭ, but that refers to branding the Mudr─Бs.[^FNB000548]

Even though there can be no fault in wearing the Mudr─Б of the blessed conch, who is an eternal associate and the best of Bh─Бgavatas, still, considering the demonic birth of the conch, as it descended with the name P─Б├▒cajanya into the womb of an Asura in order to fulfil the curse of a certain Br─Бhmaс╣Зa whose wife had had a miscarriage hearing its sound, some Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas do not wear this sign on its own or separately. This opinion the author presents here.

┬│тБ░┬╣The intelligent one should in this way wear the disc and so on using blessed Gop─лcandana every day, but on days such as ┼Ъayana, it is also said that they should be branded.

Broo

They, the disc and so on, should be branded or burned with brands correctly heated in fire on days such as ┼Ъayana Dv─Бda┼Ы─л, Utth─Бna Dv─Бda┼Ы─л and so on. The implied meaning is that since the author is now describing the daily rites, the rules for that are not given here. It is said is used to indicate the evidence for this practice given by statements of both the ┼Ъruti and the Smс╣Ыti.

Characteristics of the Disc and so on

┬│тБ░┬▓The disc should be a hexagon with twelve spokes surrounded by three rings. Blessed HariтАЩs conch turns to the right. ┬│тБ░┬│The opinion of the wise is that the club, lotus and so on are well-known. The Mudr─Б should be marked with the LordтАЩs name or with the mantra of eight-syllables or another.[^FNB000549]

Well-known: they have the form that is seen in the world. It should be marked with the LordтАЩs name such as Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, R─Бma and so on or with the mantra of eight syllables or another such as the five-syllable one.[^FNB000550]

Wearing M─Бl─Бs and so on

┬│тБ░тБ┤Then one should wear M─Бl─Бs offered to Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa made of Tulas─л leaves, lotus seeds, Tulas─л wood or Dh─Бtr─л fruits.[^FNB000551] ┬│тБ░тБ╡A Vaiс╣гс╣Зava should also wear ornaments of Tulas─л wood on the head, ears, arms or cubits according to his taste.

[тАж]

Wearing the marks of Viс╣гс╣Зu and using the voice for glorifying his names should here be understood as examples [of the signs of a Vaiс╣гс╣Зava]. Similar cases elsewhere should be considered in the same way.

According to the statement of the blessed Lord in the Viс╣гс╣Зudharmottara Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000558]

┬│┬╣тБ╣One who wears a M─Бl─Б of Tulas─л wood around the neck will without a doubt come to me, even if he is unclean or lacks good conduct.

In the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (2.5.4.3тАУ5):[^FNB000559]

┬│┬▓тБ░The one on whose body one can see a M─Бl─Б of Dh─Бtr─л fruits and Tulas─л wood is the best of Bh─Бgavatas. ┬│┬▓┬╣One who wear a M─Бl─Б of Tulas─л leaves that has been carried by Viс╣гс╣Зu around the neck, is especially honoured by the gods. ┬│┬▓┬▓A M─Бl─Б of Tulas─л leaves or one made of Dh─Бtr─л fruits gives liberation to the sinners, not to mention the servants of Viс╣гс╣Зu!

[тАж]

In connection with K─Бrttika in the same book (2.4.12.78, 80тАУ81[^FNB000560]):

┬│┬▓┬│One who wears a Tulas─л M─Бl─Б around the neck and worships Jan─Бrdana attains for every [offered] flower the merit of ten thousand cows. ┬│┬▓тБ┤As long as a Dh─Бtr─л M─Бl─Б dangles from the neck of a human being, so long Ke┼Ыava will lovingly dance within his body. ┬│┬▓тБ╡As many body hairs of humans as a Dh─Бtr─л M─Бl─Б touches in the age of Kali, for so many thousands of years will one live in the abode of Ke┼Ыava. ┬│┬▓тБ╢As many days as a human being wears a Dh─Бtr─л M─Бl─Б in the age of Kali, for so many thousands of Yugas will he live in Vaikuс╣Зс╣нha. ┬│┬▓тБ╖And one who always wears two M─Бl─Бs around the neckтАФone of Dh─Бtr─л and one of TulasiтАФwill stay in heaven for ten million Kalpas.

Rules for Performing Sandhy─Б at Home

┬│┬│тБ╢One should then perform the rituals connected with the Sandhy─Б worship in the proper way and there offer libations to the gods and others only with water from Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣ЗaтАЩs feet.

Sandhy─Б worship was described in connection to bathing at a T─лrtha earlier on (3.308тАУ353). Now the author describes it in relation to [worship at] the home. There means in the context of this ritual.

As it is said in the Skanda Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):[^FNB000562]

┬│┬│тБ╖For Vaiс╣гс╣Зavas, to keep that which has been offered to Viс╣гс╣Зu on the head and to offer libations to the forefathers and the gods with his foot water is considered the same.

That which has been offered to Viс╣гс╣Зu means that which is flowing from him. These two actions are known to be the same or equal.

In connection with Sandhy─Б worship, there is this statement by Vasiс╣гс╣нha (тАУ):[^FNB000563]

┬│┬│тБ╕Sandhy─Б in the home is one unit; in a cow pasture, it is known as tenfold; in a river, a hundred- or thousandfold; and unlimited in the shrine of Viс╣гс╣Зu.

Worship of the Blessed Guru

┬│┬│тБ╣In order to then worship Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, one should first bow down to the preceptor if present and worship him after giving him some offering.

As it is said in the Smс╣Ыtimah─Бrс╣Зava:[^FNB000564]

┬│тБ┤тБ░One should not see a king, a physician or a preceptor empty-handed; one should not see a son, a disciple or a servant with a gift.

Broo

[тАж]

Moreover, according to the statement of the blessed Lord:[^FNB000565]

┬│тБ┤┬╣One should first worship the preceptor and then also myself. Doing so one attains perfection; doing otherwise will be fruitless.

Now, after including here a statement testifying that one should offer some kind of a gift, the author now proves with statements of the blessed Lord and so on in verses341тАУ342 that one should first worship the preceptor if he is present. [тАж]

And according to the statement of N─Бrada:[^FNB000566]

┬│тБ┤┬▓But one who in the presence of the preceptor first worships someone else will attain a bad destination; his worship is fruitless.

The Greatness of the Blessed Guru

In the ┼Ъruti (┼Ъvet─Б┼Ыvatara Upaniс╣гad 6.23):

┬│тБ┤┬│To one who has the highest devotion to the Lord, and as the Lord, so also to the preceptor, the great ones will reveal all of these things.

Things means goals of human life.

In the words of the blessed Lord in the Eleventh Book (BhP11.17.27):[^FNB000567]

┬│тБ┤тБ┤One should understand the preceptor as me and never disrespect him. One should never murmur at him, thinking him a human, for the preceptor embodies all the gods.

Murmur at means find faults.

And in the Tenth Book (BhP10.80.34):[^FNB000568]

┬│тБ┤тБ╡I, the self of all beings, am not as pleased by worship, initiation, penance or calmness as by service to the preceptor.

Worship means sacrifice, the Dharma of the householder. Initiation means investiture with the sacred thread; by this the Dharma of the student is indicated. Penance is the Dharma of the forest hermit and calmness is the Dharma of the renunciant. I, the supreme Lord, am not as pleased by these things as I am by service to the preceptor, even though I am the self of all beings.[^FNB000569]

According to the statement of N─Бrada in the Seventh Book (BhP7.15.26):[^FNB000570]

┬│тБ┤тБ╢All the studies of one who false considers the preceptor, the Lord himself and the giver of the light of knowledge, as a mortal being, are like the bathing of an elephant.

In this verse the author confirms the importance of devotion to the preceptor by showing how not having devotion towards the preceptor is the greatest of offences. [тАж] Studies means reading of the scriptures. The meaning of the bathing of an elephant is useless.[^FNB000571]

He also says this somewhere else:[^FNB000572]

┬│тБ┤тБ╖The gods diminish the practitionerтАЩs devotion to the preceptor, because the disciple will by his firm devotion to the preceptor overtake us and go to Viс╣гс╣Зu.

In the Manu Smс╣Ыti (2.153):[^FNB000573]

┬│тБ┤тБ╕One who is ignorant is a child and a giver of a mantra is a father; therefore, they call the ignorant тАЬchildтАЭ and the giver of the mantra, тАЬfatherтАЭ.

Broo

┬│тБ╡тБ╡If I have the same faith towards the preceptor as I have devotion unto Hari, then by this truth, may Hari reveal himself to me.

In the ─Аditya Pur─Бс╣Зa:[^FNB000579]

┬│тБ╡тБ╢Ignorant or learned, the guru is Jan─Бrdana. Situated on the path or not, the guru alone is always the goal.

And elsewhere:[^FNB000580]

┬│тБ╡тБ╖When Hari is angry, the guru can save, but when the guru is angry, nobody. Therefore by all efforts one should propitiate the guru alone.

In the Brahmavaivarta Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬│тБ╡тБ╕Even if beating and cursing, hostile and angry, the gurus are worshipable. One should bow to them and bring them home.

The gurus are in the plural for the sake of respect, or else in order to incidentally include other elders [gurus] as well. They are described in the K┼лrma Pur─Бс╣Зa (2.12.26тАУ27ab, 31cdтАУ32ab): тАЬThe teacher, the father, the eldest brother, the king, the maternal uncle, the father-in-law, the mother,[^FNB000581] the maternal and paternal grandfathers, the Br─Бhmaс╣Зa and the paternal uncleтАФall of these are known as elders. And of all elders, five are especially worshipable, and of them, the three first are the main ones, and among them, the mother is most highly honoured.тАЭ And also (2.12.32cdтАУ34ab): тАЬHe who gives life, she who gives birth, the one who imparts knowledge, the eldest brother and the masterтАФthese five are elders. One who desires welfare should worship especially these five with all effort, even to the extent of giving up oneтАЩs life.тАЭ

┬│тБ╡тБ╣Praiseworthy that life, happy that day and propitious that moment when one approaches the preceptor with devotion and bows to him.

Broo

And also:

┬│тБ╢тБ░Even vultures do not care for the dead bodies of those ungrateful wretches who give up a traditional teacher. ┬│тБ╢┬╣By doing so, one spoils oneтАЩs insight and demonstrates oneтАЩs wickedness. One who rejects the preceptor has already rejected Hari.

And elsewhere:

┬│тБ╢┬▓That lowest of men who after attaining a preceptor through folly turns away from him up is boiled in hell for millions of Kalpas.

By showing how rejecting the preceptor is the greatest of offences, the author in verses360тАУ362 confirms the greatness of the preceptor. Traditional means one descended in a family line or one enjoined by the Veda. Insight means knowledge or wisdom. Attaining a preceptor means having accepted him as oneтАЩs preceptor.

The Exception to This

In the Pa├▒car─Бtra:[^FNB000582]

┬│тБ╢┬│A mantra given by a non-Vaiс╣гс╣Зava will lead one to hell. According to the rules one should again properly take it from a Vaiс╣гс╣Зava guru.

By giving verses such as тАЬIgnorant or learned тАжтАЭ (4.356) or тАЬEven vultures тАжтАЭ (4.360), the author has stated that the preceptor is in no way to be rejected. Now, what if by mistake one has accepted a non-Vaiс╣гс╣Зava preceptor? In that case, he is to be rejected. This is the context of the exception given here to the previous statements. The causative form of take (gr─Бhayet) should be taken as simply тАЬtakeтАЭ. Or else it means that the saintly persons will mercifully cause the mantra to be taken by such a person. It is to be understood that one should accept the mantra from a Vaiс╣гс╣Зava and generally from a Br─Бhmaс╣Зa, as was written above in connection with the qualities of the preceptor (1.47тАУ54).

The Result of Not Devoting Oneself to the Guru

In the Agastya Saс╣Гhit─Б (8.24, 26тАУ28):

┬│тБ╢тБ┤Greatest of sages! There is no rescue from the suffering of hell for those sinful wretches, the lowest of men, who does not fulfil the order of the preceptor. ┬│тБ╢тБ╡For disciples who disrespect their preceptors when they should always be honoured, will be bereft of such blessings as sons, friends and wives. ┬│тБ╢тБ╢Those who by mistake insult the preceptor or engage in abusive words will be born as pigs for hundreds of lifetimes. ┬│тБ╢тБ╖Those fools who harm the preceptor always engage in sin; without a doubt all their good deeds turn to sins.

Having confirmed the importance of devotion to the blessed preceptor, the author in verses364тАУ367 describes the faults of hell for those who do not have devotion to him. Therefore they always engage in sin.

┬│тБ╢тБ╖Then, after honouring the preceptor thinking him to be Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, the intelligent one should bow to him like a stick fallen to the ground three or more uneven times.

About this, there is the statement of Vy─Бsa in the K┼лrma Pur─Бс╣Зa (тАУ):

┬│тБ╢тБ╣One should grasp the guru with crossed arms, touching the left with the left and the right with the right.

[тАж] Grasp means that one should take hold of his blessed feet. He explains how to do so in the next line. The meaning is that one should touch the preceptorтАЩs left foot with oneтАЩs own left hand. Similar places below should be understood in the same way.

┬│тБ╖тБ░Then, after the practitioner has received the permission of the blessed preceptors, he should, before entering the house of Hari that was cleansed earlier, take off his shoes.

Broo

The plural in the blessed preceptors is for the sake of respect. The practitioner means the worshipper of the blessed Lord. Before entering means when about to go into. The meaning is that he should leave off his shoes far from the fireplace and so on before entering.

Accordingly, ─Аpastambha says (9.20):[^FNB000583]

┬│тБ╖┬╣One should remove the shoes at a fireplace, in a cow pasture, in the presence of gods or Br─Бhmaс╣Зas, while reciting mantras and at the time of eating.

┬│тБ╖┬▓Then, having entered the yard of the temple for worshipping the blessed Lord, one should wash hands and feet and do two ─Аcamanas.

Accordingly, in the M─Бrkaс╣Зс╕Нeya Pur─Бс╣Зa (31.64cdтАУ65ab):[^FNB000584]

┬│тБ╖┬│Rituals of worshipping the gods and so on and greeting the preceptor should be done after having completely performed ─Аcamaс╣Зa; so also when conferring favours.

Completely performed ─Аcamaс╣Зa communicates that one should do two ─Аcamaс╣Зas, and that for the sake of completeness.

Thus ends the fourth chapter of the Bhagavadbhaktivil─Бsa of ┼Ъr─л Gop─Бla Bhaс╣нс╣нa, called тАЬOn the Ornaments of the Vaiс╣гс╣ЗavasтАЭ.
